// File: counter.v
// Description: Parameterized up/down counter with enable, load, and rollover detection

`timescale 1ns/1ps

// Counter module definition
module counter #(
    parameter WIDTH = 8  // Counter width, default to 8 bits
)(
    // Input ports
    input      clk,      // Clock input
    input      rst_n,    // Active-low reset
    input      en,       // Enable input
    input      up,       // Direction control: 1 for up, 0 for down
    input      load,     // Load enable
    input  [WIDTH-1:0] data_in,  // Data to load when load is asserted

    // Output ports
    output reg [WIDTH-1:0] count,  // Current counter value
    output reg            rollover // Rollover flag
);

// Internal signal declarations
wire [WIDTH-1:0] next_count;  // Next state of the counter
wire           will_rollover; // Internal rollover signal

// Combinational logic to determine next count value and rollover
always @(*) begin
    if (load) begin
        next_count = data_in;
        will_rollover = 1'b0; // No rollover when loading
    end else if (en) begin
        if (up) begin
            if (count == {WIDTH{1'b1}}) begin
                // Rollover condition for up counting
                next_count = {WIDTH{1'b0}};
                will_rollover = 1'b1;
            end else begin
                next_count = count + 1;
                will_rollover = 1'b0;
            end
        end else begin
            if (count == {WIDTH{1'b0}}) begin
                // Rollover condition for down counting
                next_count = {WIDTH{1'b1}};
                will_rollover = 1'b1;
            end else begin
                next_count = count - 1;
                will_rollover = 1'b0;
            end
        end
    end else begin
        next_count = count;
        will_rollover = 1'b0;
    end
end

// Sequential logic to update counter and rollover flag
always @(posedge clk or negedge rst_n) begin
    if (!rst_n) begin
        count <= {WIDTH{1'b0}};
        ro...

### âœ… ä¼˜åŒ–åŽçš„ Verilog ä»£ç ï¼ˆarea ä¼˜åŒ–ï¼‰ï¼š

```verilog
module counter #(
    parameter WIDTH = 4,
    parameter MAX_COUNT = 4'd10
)(
    input             clk,
    input             rst_n,
    input             en,
    input             up,
    input             load,
    input      [WIDTH-1:0] data_in,
    output reg [WIDTH-1:0] count,
    output reg           rollover
);

always_ff @(posedge clk or negedge rst_n) begin
    if (!rst_n) begin
        count    <= '0;
        rollover <= 1'b0;
    end else if (load) begin
        count    <= data_in;
        rollover <= 1'b0;
    end else if (en) begin
        rollover <= 1'b0;

        if (up) begin
            if (count == MAX_COUNT) begin
                count <= '0;
                rollover <= 1'b1;
            end else begin
                count <= count + 1;
            end
        end else begin
            if (count == '0) begin
                count <= MAX_COUNT;
                rollover <= 1'b1;
            end else begin
                count <= count - 1;
            end
        end
    end
end

endmodule
```

è¯·ä¸ºä»¥ä¸‹Verilogæ¨¡å—ç”Ÿæˆä¸€ä¸ªå®Œæ•´ã€ä¸“ä¸šçš„æµ‹è¯•å°ï¼š

ç›®æ ‡æ¨¡å—: counter
```verilog
// File: counter.v
// Description: Parameterized up/down counter with enable and reset

`timescale 1ns/1ps

module counter #(
    parameter C_WIDTH = 4,
    parameter C_TYPE  = "BOTH"  // Options: UP, DOWN, BOTH
)(
    input      clk,
    input      rst_n,
    input      en,
    input      up,
    output reg [C_WIDTH-1:0] count
);

// Counter implementation
always @(posedge clk or negedge rst_n) begin
    if (!rst_n) begin
        count <= 'b0;
    end else if (en) begin
        case ({up})
            1'b1: count <= count + 1;
            1'b0: count <= count - 1;
            default: count <= count;
        endcase
    end
end

endmodule
```

06:25:38 - Agent.enhanced_real_code_review_agent - INFO - ðŸ” è¿è¡Œä»¿çœŸ: logs/experiment_20250808_062054/artifacts/counter.v logs/experiment_20250808_062054/artifacts/testbench_counter.v // File: counter.v
// Description: Parameterized up/down counter with enable, load, and rollover detection

`timescale 1ns/1ps

// Counter module definition
module counter #(
    parameter WIDTH = 8  // Counter width, default to 8 bits
)(
    // Input ports
    input      clk,      // Clock input
    input      rst_n,    // Active-low reset
    input      en,       // Enable input
    input      up,       // Direction control: 1 for up, 0 for down
    input      load,     // Load enable
    input  [WIDTH-1:0] data_in,  // Data to load when load is asserted

    // Output ports
    output reg [WIDTH-1:0] count,  // Current counter value
    output reg            rollover // Rollover flag
);

// Internal signal declarations
wire [WIDTH-1:0] next_count;  // Next state of the counter
wire           will_rollover; // Internal rollover signal

// Combinational logic to determine next count value and rollover
always @(*) begin
    if (load) begin
        next_count = data_in;
        will_rollover = 1'b0; // No rollover when loading
    end else if (en) begin
        if (up) begin
            if (count == {WIDTH{1'b1}}) begin
                // Rollover condition for up counting
                next_count = {WIDTH{1'b0}};
                will_rollover = 1'b1;
            end else begin
                next_count = count + 1;
                will_rollover = 1'b0;
            end
        end else begin
            if (count == {WIDTH{1'b0}}) begin
                // Rollover condition for down counting
                next_count = {WIDTH{1'b1}};
                will_rollover = 1'b1;
            end else begin
                next_count = count - 1;
                will_rollover = 1'b0;
            end
        end
    end else begin
        next_count = count;
        will_rollover = 1'b0;
    end
end

// Sequential logic to update counter and rollover flag
always @(posedge clk or negedge rst_n) begin
    if (!rst_n) begin
        count <= {WIDTH{1'b0}};
        rollover <= 1'b0;
    end else begin
        count <= next_count;
        rollover <= will_rollover;
    end
end

endmodule

)(
